NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

PUBLIC NOTICES
 
D. Palraj, a male child, son of Thiru R. Durairaj, born on 7th August 1984 residing at No. 7/68, A Colony,
Chinnavedampatti, Coimbatore-641 049, has been living as female. I have granted Identity Card No. CBE/038/2018, issued by
Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. By this, I may be treated as a female and
shall henceforth be known as D. AKSHAYA.
Coimbatore, 
D. PALRAJ
15th March 2021.

Card No. CHN/012/2019, issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. By this,
I may be treated as a Trans women and shall henceforth be known as G.  SAMBAVI
Chennai, 
G. SAMBASIVAM
18th March 2021.
